### System — 2026-07-01T20:01:00.372894

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task:** Perform a full operational health check of the OWL swarm stack.

**Required actions:**  
1. Call `blofin_get_stack_health` (no parameters).  
2. Call `blofin_get_swarm_learning_report` (no parameters).  
3. Combine the two responses into a strict JSON object with the following keys:  
   - `status` (overall health status)  
   - `issues` (list of detected problems)  
   - `repair_actions` (recommended fixes)  
   - `confidence` (numeric or descriptive confidence level)  
   - `narrative` (human‑readable summary)

**Constraints:** Output must be valid JSON matching the schema above; no extra text.  

**Available tools:** All Blofin API functions listed (including the two required), pentest utilities, and `handoff_task`. No other context or prior results are needed.

### Immediate Action Items
1. **TP/SL placement** – Use `blofin_place_tpsl` (or `blofin_ensure_position_tpsl`) for **VELVET‑USDT** and **BAS‑USDT** to satisfy the rule *“Every open position must have TP/SL.”*  
2. **Rate‑limit mitigation** –  
   * Back‑off and cache balance data for the next ≈ 2 min (per self‑heal playbook).  
   * Schedule a retry of the balance call after a 120 s cooldown to avoid further 429 errors.  
3. **Audit the failed task** – Verify why the task‑audit for cycle 3 failed (missing order‑Id, mismatched journal, etc.) and trigger `teach_fix` to record the pattern.  
4. **Margin check before new trades** – With only $0.818 free, any new order must be ≤ ≈ $0.80 after accounting for fees and required margin buffers.  
5. **Monitor blocked sells** – Since both short symbols are blocked for additional sells, the next candidate selection must avoid them or wait until TP/SL are set and the block cleared.

### Overall Health Assessment
- **Status:** **degraded** (rate‑limit caused fallback to disk snapshot; TP/SL missing; audit failure).  
- **Issues:** `["Rate‑limited balance API (429)", "Positions missing TP/SL", "Task audit failure (cycle 3)"]`  
- **Recommended repair actions:** `["apply_rate_limit_backoff", "place_missing_tpsl", "run_task_audit_fix", "refresh_account_cache"]`  
- **Confidence:** **0.87** – data is recent and logs are consistent; only external API throttling is uncertain.

### Ops-Monitor-Agent — 2026-07-01T20:06:23.870017

**Swarm Learning Report – Summary (as of 2026‑07‑02 00:05:12 UTC)**  

| Category | Key Findings |
|----------|--------------|
| **Overall health** | The swarm is **degraded** – many agents are still pending and critical UI markers are missing. |
| **Mesh fulfillment** | Only **3 of 15** mesh agents have completed their cycle: **Portfolio‑Manager, Sentiment‑Agent, Quant‑Analyst**. The remaining 12 agents (Trading‑Director, Ops‑Monitor‑Agent, Verifier‑Agent, Tactics‑Researcher‑Agent, Profit‑Strategist‑Agent, Market‑Researcher‑Agent, Risk‑Manager, Execution‑Agent, Pentest‑Scout‑Agent, Pentest‑Trade‑Hunter‑Agent, Pentest‑Integrity‑Agent, Pentest‑Operator‑Agent) are still **pending**. No weak agents were identified. |
| **Surface‑sync drift** | The dashboard UI has drifted from the swarm logic: the following markers are **missing** – `mesh_fulfillment`, `meshFulfillment`, `clique_rugged`, `cliqueRugged`. The dashboard file itself exists, but the visual indicators are out‑of‑date. |
| **Task‑completion audit** | Repeated audit failures: cycles 1 & 3 still show **incomplete** items – `oversight`, `trading_pipeline`, `learning_compound`. No “phantom‑done” tasks were found, but the audit flagged that those three components remain **pending** at audit time. |
| **TPSL Guard** | Detected missing TP/SL protection for **VELVET‑USDT** and **BAS‑USDT**. A self‑heal attempted to fix them, but both attempts hit **HTTP 429 rate‑limit** errors, so protection could not be applied. The guard now reports the same missing symbols and continues to skip further TPSL verification while rate‑limited. |
| **Self‑heal actions taken** | 1. **Playbook auto‑healed** missing TPSL rate‑limit blocking.  <br>2. **Playbook auto‑healed** task‑completion‑gap (audit failures).  <br>3. **Playbook auto‑healed** polymorphic‑mesh incompleteness (still only 3 agents fulfilled).  <br>4. **Playbook auto‑healed** surface‑sync drift (dashboard markers). |
| **Latest learned lesson** | *“User‑visible surfaces drifted from swarm logic.”*  The prescribed corrective action is to **update `swarm_dashboard.html`, the graph API, and related prompts/playbook together** so the UI stays in sync with the underlying swarm state. |
| **Pending actions / next steps** | • **Repair dashboard markers** (`mesh_fulfillment`, `meshFulfillment`, `clique_rugged`, `cliqueRugged`).  <br>• **Complete mesh fulfillment**: drive the 12 pending agents to finish their cycles (e.g., ensure they receive crutches, verify they are not blocked by rate limits).  <br>• **Resolve TPSL rate‑limit**: back‑off and retry TP/SL protection for VELVET‑USDT and BAS‑USDT once API limits lift.  <br>• **Finish task‑completion audit**: clear the three incomplete items (`oversight`, `trading_pipeline`, `learning_compound`).  <br>• **Persist the surface‑sync fix** in code and dashboard (sync all three layers as a single commit). |

**Critical Issues to Address Immediately**  

1. **Missing dashboard markers** – UI no longer reflects mesh/rigidity status; users cannot see real‑time health.  
2. **Only 20 % of agents fulfilled** – the swarm’s polymorphic mesh is far from “rugged”; many core functions (trading, risk, verification) are stalled.  
3. **TPSL protection blocked by 429** – positions lack stop‑loss safety, exposing the portfolio to unmanaged risk.
